The Great Cultural Promotion in the Modern National Medicine News 63

The Chinese Medicine Bookstore is the only institution in the National Medicine field...Special prices from July 1st

The Chinese Medicine World is the only publication in the National Medicine field...National Medicine professionals should subscribe

The Chinese Medicine Bookstore, located at No. 13 Shandong Road in this city, was founded by well-known figures in the medical and literary circles of Shanghai. It was established on June 3, 1929. In just two years, it has published as many as 150 kinds of books. These published books are all the elite masterpieces of famous doctors from ancient and modern times, gathered in one place. It has made particular efforts to publish Japanese works, such as the published Annotations and Commentaries on the Classic of Difficulties, Ancient Meaning of the Classic of Difficulties, Wing Recipes of the Treatise on Cold Damage, Identification of Essentials of the Treatise on Cold Damage, Materia Medica for the Medicine Basket, Medicine Tax, Selected Emergency Recipes, and Examination of Vomiting Recipes, etc., no less than dozens of kinds, all of which are valuable works by famous doctors of the Han Dynasty, such as Todo Yoshimasu, Tanba Motoyasu, Kuri Sono, and Asada, etc. The director of the editorial department of the bookstore is Mr. Qin Bowei, who is currently the honorary director of the Central National Medical Museum, a standing committee member of the National Medical Association, and holds important positions in dozens of other medical and pharmaceutical organizations and medical schools. His moral character and literary talent have long been admired by people from all walks of life. Therefore, the Chinese Medicine World, which he edits, is known as the champion of national Chinese medicine magazines, and its reputation overflows the medical field. Its value can be imagined. The fourteenth issue of the third volume of the magazine has been published, and the articles published are all written by famous doctors from China. The annual subscription for twelve issues is only one dollar and fifty cents. Anyone who subscribes to the magazine can purchase books from the bookstore with the subscription form. In this city, a 10% discount will be given on the actual price. In other cities, postage will be waived. If you purchase fifteen dollars worth of books from the bookstore within a year, a 10% discount will be given or one dollar and fifty cents will be deducted from the postage. This magazine fee can be recovered, and you will also receive complimentary copies from the Chinese medicine publishing industry on a regular basis. Isn't this wonderful? It can be seen that the promotion of Chinese medicine culture is a vigorous and enthusiastic promotion of national medicine. This time, for the third anniversary of the start of business, in addition to the three-day special price that was held last time, we are now sacrificing money and effort to make a larger promotion and popularize national Chinese medicine education with a special price for one month. Whether you buy a lot or a little of books from July 1st to July 31st, you will receive preferential treatment.

Official Presents the Title and Seal, Xue presents the title and seal to the Chairman, the Chairman reads the full text of the title-conferring document, (10) (1) The Chairman personally confers the title and seal. Panchen Erdeni steps forward to receive them reverently. (10) (2) Panchen Erdeni bows once to the Chairman. (Panchen hands the title and seal to the Kambo and retreats three steps, stopping and bowing.) (10) (3) Panchen Erdeni respectfully presents a Hada. (The interpreter presents the Hada to Panchen, and the Chairman accepts it and hands it to the title-conferring official.) (10) (4) The Chairman presents a Hada in return (The official presenting the seal presents the Hada to the Chairman, Panchen accepts it and hands it to the interpreter.) (10) (5) The Chairman delivers a speech. (10) (6) Panchen Erdeni responds with thanks. (10) (7) Music is played. (10) (8) The ceremony is completed. (10) (9) A photograph is taken.

Title Conferring Ceremony (1) Participating personnel on the day of the title conferring ceremony include civil officials of the government at the recommended level or above and military officers at the rank of major or above; civil officials of various agencies at the simplified level or above and military officers at the rank of colonel or above. (2) Personnel participating in the title-conferring ceremony must wear formal attire. Panchen Erdeni and his accompanying Kambos must wear Tibetan formal attire. (3) The title-conferring ceremony must have various officials responsible for the ceremony, designated by the Bureau of Ceremonies. (4) Panchen Erdeni, leading two Kambos and participating personnel, must gather in the National Government Reception Room before the stipulated time. At that time, the Director of the Bureau of Ceremonies will lead them into the auditorium to hold the title-conferring ceremony according to the prescribed order. (5) After the ceremony and photography, the Director of the Bureau of Ceremonies will lead Panchen Erdeni into the interview room. The Chief of Civilian Affairs, Chief Military Counselor, Minister of the Interior, and Chairman of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission will meet him. Erdeni bows once to the Chairman. After the ceremony, he sits down. The Chairman sits in the middle, with the Chief of Civilian Affairs, Chief Military Counselor, Minister of the Interior, and Chairman of the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission sitting on the left and right. Panchen Erdeni sits opposite. After the Chairman speaks, Panchen Erdeni bows once to the Chairman and withdraws.

Chairman's Speech The speech briefly states that the Republic of China is based on the spirit of equality among the five races to build a national government. The provisional constitution during the period of political tutelage is based on the principles of national freedom and equality to enhance the faith of all people. Panchen Master has always supported the Central Government and has made great efforts to study the Three Principles of the People and to publicize them as much as possible. The government has relied on him deeply, so it has specially bestowed him with a laudatory title and conferred upon him the title and seal in a grand ceremony. Today happens to be the sixth anniversary of the founding of the National Government. Recalling that the late Premier Sun Yat-sen aimed to seek universal happiness for the Chinese nation and all mankind with the doctrine of saving people, saving the country, and saving the world, so that they could jointly enjoy the benefits of the Three Principles of the People, it is hoped that the Master will vigorously promote the late Premier's great doctrine to achieve assimilation, so as to permanently lay the foundation of the Three Principles of the People and the nation, thereby living up to the government's expectations. This is what is greatly hoped for.

Panchen's Response Panchen has been in the East for nine years. Fortunately, our Chairman unified the North and South and laid the foundation for the country, so I was able to respectfully visit the capital and pay my respects. My private joy cannot be described. As the National Government is implementing the late Premier Sun Yat-sen's teachings, it convened the National Assembly, and I was able to participate in the grand meeting, which was a great honor. Furthermore, I am grateful to the government for considering my humble sincerity and bestowing upon me a laudatory title. Today, I come to the government to receive it, which only increases my shame and trepidation. From now on, I will only fulfill the inherent function of religion, pray sincerely, protect the country's foundation in lasting peace, promote far-reaching cultural education, use a long tongue to translate and explain the Three Principles of the People, enlighten and awaken people's minds, and convert the Mongolian and Tibetan people through party education. I vow to devote all my loyalty to repay a drop of kindness. I humbly offer my foolish sincerity to express my thanks and sincerity.

Full text of the title conferred: Broadly gathering the red universe, knowing the subtle is also knowing the manifest, widely transforming Qian Pi, possessing virtue is possessing the multitude, Panchen Erdeni, pacifying and uniting Tibet, supporting the Central Government, spreading education to the original people, serving the Republic of China, truly explaining the wonderful truth, richly receiving supreme honor, should be conferred the title of National Protector, Propagator of Buddhism, Broad Wisdom Master, illuminating the wish-fulfilling pearl, carrying out the great mandate, virtuous words spread everywhere, proclaiming the grand plans of the Three Principles of the People and the Five Powers, the legal bell is clearly displayed, illustrating the wonderful functions of the six degrees and ten thousand practices, reverently obeying the grand canon, further promoting religious customs, Chairman of the National Government Chiang Kai-shek.

Gifts Presented When Panchen bid farewell at around 11:00 AM, Ma Fuxiang, Liu Shangqing, Ye Chucang, and He Yaozu escorted him to the second gate of the National Government and specially presented a pair of enamel silver tripods, eight pieces of tribute satin, four pieces of colored silk, and two pairs of embroidered hanging screens, and sent personnel to deliver them to Panchen's residence.

Panchen's Attire On that day, Panchen wore a purple kasaya, slightly revealing a round collar, a gold-threaded brocade formal dress, and white felt boots. The sides of the boots were lined with purple, gold, and red satin. The attire was quite peculiar. He wore glasses on his nose.

Jiangxi Province Orders General Offensive to Suppress Bandits 64

He Yingqin Arrives in Fuzhou from Nanchang

Nanchang Dispatch: After Chairman Jiang arrived in Jiangxi, arrangements for bandit suppression were already in place. The various important news items are recorded below:

He Yingqin Departs for Fuzhou: Commander-in-Chief He Yingqin, upon receiving orders to proceed to Fuzhou to supervise the troops, visited Jiang at the military headquarters on the morning of the 28th to seek instructions. He then went to the Provincial Government and Provincial Party Headquarters to bid farewell. At around 11 a.m., he led Chief of Staff He and other personnel from various departments, traveling in several cars, to the riverbank. They boarded a steamer to depart. Lu Diping, Xiong Shihui, Cao Haosen, all members of the Provincial Party Headquarters and Provincial Government, and representatives of various people's organizations were already at the riverbank to see him off. After He got out of the car, he shook hands with everyone present, then boarded the Qinghe steamer and set sail, heading up the Fu River towards Fuzhou. Yu Feipeng and others accompanied him. Yu was going to supervise logistics and military supplies. On the 29th, He arrived safely in Fuzhou. The date for the general offensive is expected to be soon.

Lai and Li Arrive in Jiangxi Together: Lai Xinhui arrived in the province from Hankou a few days ago and immediately met with Chairman Jiang to report on the situation in Yichang and Hankou, and to request instructions on matters in Sichuan. Li Mingzhong and Fang Boren have also recently arrived in Jiangxi from Hankou. After Li arrived, he reported to Jiang on the bandit situation along the borders of Sichuan, Hubei, and Hunan, and requested instructions and advice. Fang came at the invitation to assist in military operations and will serve at the military headquarters.

Hunan Generals Arrive in Jiangxi for Instructions: Liu Jianxu, Li Jue, Tao Guang, and others arrived in Jiangxi from Hunan on the 29th. As soon as they arrived, they went to the military headquarters to meet with Jiang. Liu reported on the bandit suppression situation in Pingjiang, Liuyang, Lingxian, and Guixian, as well as the border defenses of Hunan, Guangdong, and Guangxi, and the recent military and political situation in Hunan. Jiang expressed great satisfaction and gave them instructions. It is said that Liu and others will return to Hunan on July 2nd to report to He Jian, so that Peng Weiren and various division commanders can come to Jiangxi to receive instructions from Jiang.

Tu Weifan Arrested and Punished: Tu Weifan (Deputy Commander of the 52nd Division), former commander of the Nanchang Garrison and concurrently head of the Security Office, was reported to the military headquarters by the people for various illegal activities. Jiang removed Tu from all his positions and appointed Lu Diping as the garrison commander and Sun Changjun as the head of the Security Office. He also ordered the military headquarters to arrest Tu and hand him over to the military court for strict punishment in accordance with the law, to maintain military discipline and to deter others. After Lu was appointed garrison commander, he scheduled to take office on July 1st and decided to expand the organization, dividing it into four departments: staff, adjutant, detention and investigation, and law enforcement. It is said that Xie Muhan will be appointed as Chief of Staff, and Wang Shihe, the Chief of the Bodyguard of the Headquarters, will concurrently serve as the Head of the Detention and Investigation Department. Lu sent people on the 28th to take over the files and equipment of the former Garrison Headquarters.

Aviation Office Added to the Headquarters: At around 11 a.m. on the 26th, Huang Bingheng, Director of the Central Aviation Administration, led squadron leader Zhang Tingmeng and others to Jiangxi on the Yongke aircraft. Chairman Jiang, considering that many combat and reconnaissance aircraft have arrived in the province, and that airfields have been built in Fuzhou, Ji'an, Jiujiang, Ganzhou, and other places, has added an Aviation Office to the headquarters for the purpose of unified command. Mao Bangchu, Principal of the Aviation School, will concurrently serve as the Director of the office. Mao has come to the province from Nanjing to take office. As for the aircraft in Jiangxi, Huang Bingheng has been supervising and directing them in reconnaissance and bombing missions, which have been very effective.

Admonition to the People and County Magistrates: Chairman Jiang believes that this bandit suppression campaign involves the integrated use of the Party, government, and military to eliminate the root of the bandits, and that it is necessary for everyone to be of one mind and for the entire population to be mobilized to succeed. He issued an open letter to the people of Jiangxi, stating that the local gentry must stand up and take responsibility, strive for righteousness for humanity, and seek security for mankind, with one heart and one mind, eliminate the red bandits, and thereby save themselves and others. In the future, information on bandit suppression strategies, local rehabilitation, official misconduct, and military discipline can be reported to the military headquarters. Zhongzheng [Jiang] will personally review and adopt them to understand the people's sentiments. He also issued an admonishing telegram to the county magistrates, stating that the county magistrates must eliminate the habit of inertia, inspire their innate loyalty and righteousness, and resolve to survive or perish with the city. If they continue to procrastinate, or seek to preserve their lives, or abandon the city upon hearing of an alarm, they will be subject to military law and sentenced to death. Even if they flee alone, their guarantors and family members will be held accountable. (June 30)

Recent Deployment of Guangdong and Guangxi Troops 65

Guangzhou Dispatch: In Guangdong province, Li Yangjing's 3rd Army, which belongs to Chen Jitang's 1st Army Group, has recently redeployed its main forces to Shaoguan and Yingde for defense. Yu Hanmou's 1st Army, Li Zhenqiu's division, is deployed in the suburbs, up to Conghua. Ye Zhao's brigade is stationed in Huaxian Juntian, connecting with Li's forces of the 3rd Army. Zengcheng, Longmen, Dongguan, and other areas are guarded by Xiang Hanping's 2nd Army. Huizhou, Pingshan, Danshui, Sanduozhu, and other places are defended by Huang Renhuan's Independent 1st Division. However, the defense line along the Dong River is weak, with only a few regiments of the 2nd Independent Division deployed in Chaozhou and Meizhou. The military authorities have long planned to reinforce this area, but there is no suitable senior officer to take charge. Recently, Xu Chongzhi resigned and has been spending his days at Li Fulin's estate in Datang Township, Henan, indifferent to current affairs. Sun Ke and others are unwilling to see Xu idle, and discussed with Chen Jitang to appoint Xu to an important military position, providing him with a certain amount of military funds each month, so that Xu can go to the Dong River or elsewhere to reorganize his old troops and form an army as soon as possible. As for weapons, it is planned to ask Chen Jitang for a loan. However, Xu has not yet agreed to this proposal. One report says that Xu intends to rise again, and his former subordinate, Sun Benrong, has scheduled to go to a certain place to recruit his old troops. This is the latest military news from the Dong River. As for the northwest river area, Chen Jitang's troops are concentrated in the suburbs of Guangzhou. If there is trouble on the border in the future, he will need the assistance of other troops. Therefore, Li Zongren has been attending military conferences in Guangzhou for days, advocating that Guangxi should deploy some troops to Guangdong for joint defense. Chen Jitang, seeing that the war has not yet broken out, has only allowed Zhang Guiji's army to prepare to mobilize a part of its forces to the area where the Xiaobei River intersects the Guangxi border, in case of emergency. He also sent Bai Chongxi back to Guangxi first to make arrangements. After Bai returned to Guangxi, he convened a military conference in Wuzhou on the evening of the 23rd. In recent days, the Guangxi troops have been slightly mobilized. Wu Qiwai's division of Zhang Fakui's army has moved east from Pingle, and most of it is waiting for orders in Hexian. If necessary, it can enter Guangdong along the Xiaobei River through Lianxian for joint defense. Also, Qi Daozheng's regiment of Huang Heling's division of the Guangxi army, and Li Mo's regiment of Li Pinxian's army, have arrived in Wuzhou in recent days. Zhou Yuan's regiment of Huang's division has moved to Tengxian, Xu Jiangguang's regiment is stationed in Mengjiang, and Lin Maomeng and Meng Zhihong's two regiments are stationed in Pingnan. Li Fawen, Wang Zhibin, and Wei Hengxin's three regiments of Li Pinxian's division are deployed in the Da Huangjiang Guiping area. In total, there are eleven regiments of Guangxi troops concentrated in Xunwu and Wuzhou, totaling approximately 13,000 people, and Zhang Fakui's entire army, approximately 8,000 people, is concentrated in Hexian. (June 27)

Hubei Department of Finance Establishes Loan 66

The Creditor is a Banking Group

The Loan Amount is 600,000

Hankou Dispatch: Since Hubei Province abolished the likin tax, the revenue from the business tax has been extremely sluggish, and the financial situation has reached a critical point. The newly appointed Director of Finance, Wu Guozhen, negotiated a large loan with the Hankou banking group. After several negotiations, a new loan of 600,000 yuan was finalized on the 29th, and a contract was signed with the Bank of China in Hankou. 100,000 silver dollars were paid immediately, and the remaining 500,000 yuan will be paid in full within the month. The loan is secured by 1.2 million yuan face value of customs tax treasury bonds and rehabilitation public bonds. The monthly interest rate is 1.2%, and the principal and interest are to be repaid from August to December, with monthly payments of 120,000 yuan allocated from the special tax agreement. As for the loan amounts from the banking group, the Provincial Bank loaned 50,000 yuan, the Bank of China 62,500 yuan, the Bank of Communications 60,000 yuan, and the Jin Cheng, Salt Industry, Continental, Central South, Zhejiang Industrial, Zhejiang Xingye, Si Ming, and Shanghai banks each loaned 45,000 yuan. The China Industrial, Ju Xingcheng, and Guangdong banks each loaned 22,500 yuan, totaling 600,000 yuan. (June 29)

Shandong Department of Education Instructs Provincial Education Bureaus to Protect Antiquities 67

Jinan Dispatch: Shandong is a land of culture, with numerous antiquities both above and below ground, all of which have cultural value. After the Gao family in Weixian sold all their collection of Qin and Han bricks and tiles to the Japanese, the Shandong Provincial Government, in order to preserve antiquities, and in accordance with the regulations issued by the central government, specially instructed the Weixian County Magistrate to severely reprimand them. Now, the Department of Education, in order to prevent further theft and sale of antiquities throughout the province, specifically instructed all provincial education bureaus to publicize the details of the private sale of bricks and tiles in Weixian, ordering all bureau directors to take proper care to protect antiquities, so as to prevent them from flowing overseas, and to avoid censure. The Department of Education also specially instructed the Weixian County Magistrate and the Director of the Education Bureau to severely reprimand them. The instructions are recorded as follows: Our country has the longest history, and the artifacts of each dynasty are made differently. By examining the changes in their quality and texture, we can see the order of evolution. Inscriptions on metal and stone are related to production and can be used to verify history. However, it is difficult to investigate and determine methods of preservation and it is impossible to avoid losses. The National Government has long recognized this and promulgated the Law on the Preservation of Antiquities, and this department has already transmitted it to all for compliance. The education authorities in all counties and cities should conscientiously comply with it to value antiquities. Recently, the Gao family in Weixian secretly sold seven boxes of Qin and Han bricks, tiles, and stone carvings out of the country. Fortunately, the Jiaoji Railway Bureau discovered and detained them. On June 14th, this department transported them all to Jinan from Qingdao. It was decided that on the 16th, the Provincial Government and this department would send personnel to jointly open and inspect the seal with the Director of the Provincial Library. A total of 531 pieces of bricks and tiles and 2 pieces of stone carvings were found. They have now been handed over to the Jinshi Conservation Institute of the Provincial Library for proper preservation. According to this item, these bricks and tiles were collected by the Gao family, which is quite precious. However, future generations do not know to cherish them, and sell them to foreigners, ignoring the overall situation. This is obviously wrong. The County Education Bureau did not detect it beforehand, and did not report it afterwards, and its handling of affairs was negligent. In addition to severely reprimanding the bureau director, and ordering the county magistrate to forward the reprimand to the Gao family, this is hereby ordered to be followed. In the future, ancient artifacts must be carefully protected and inspected at any time, so as to avoid losses and to pass them on forever. This is of utmost importance. This order.

Anti-Embankment Riot Occurs in Xuzhou 68

Xuzhou Dispatch: Before the tenth year of Xianfeng in the Qing Dynasty, Xuzhoubu was the area through which the Yellow River flowed. After the Yellow River breached the levee at Tongwaxiang and moved north, Xuzhoubu was no longer plagued by floods. Therefore, the north, east, and south sides of Xuzhou city have remains of the old Yellow River embankment, which is about ten miles long. The embankment stones are huge and long, and are joined with a mixture of rice juice and ash, making them extremely strong. After the river moved, poor people gathered on the embankment, living attached to the embankment, and making it their livelihood for a long time. In recent years, the waterways have not been dredged, and during the summer rainy season, the rivers rise. The old embankment, even though it is in disrepair, is still sufficient to prevent floods. Unexpectedly, Li Enbao, the former director of the Xuzhou Property Clearance Bureau, secretly sold the old Yellow River embankment and all the official wasteland to the Jiudetang before his term ended. It has been found that the Jiudetang is a private land company organization with nine shareholders, including Lan Haiqiu, Xi Peichen, and Wang Xiangfu. A contact point was set up outside the East Gate. In recent months, disputes have arisen from the measurement of official land. Recently, Zuo Shufu, the current Director of the Property Clearance Bureau, was assisted in measuring the river embankment, causing the residents attached to the embankment to rise up and block them. They once attacked the personnel sent by the Property Bureau. On June 29th, the County Government responded to the Property

Page 11

Summary of Important News 69

Bureau's letter and sent police to arrest Zhang Chuanyi and four other residents who had blocked the measurement of the embankment, and detained them in the county government. On the afternoon of the 30th, about three or four hundred men, women, old, and young, gathered from the nearby households, holding flags and braving the rain, and set off from the Yellow River embankment. They entered the West Gate via Yiqia Road and Yingshi Street, chanting slogans along the way to overthrow the Property Bureau and Jiudetang. Then they went to the county government to petition. The police team added posts in front of the gate and advised them to elect representatives. The crowd did not listen and broke into the gate in large numbers, smashing the dispatching office with bricks and stones. The police team could not stop them and fired warning shots into the air. The crowd retreated slightly, but due to the crowding, an old man was trampled to death. Seven or eight policemen were also injured by the people. Upon hearing the news, the Public Security Bureau sent more police to the scene to suppress the riot and arrested ten ringleaders. The rest of the crowd dispersed. County Magistrate Yang Wei immediately convened a meeting of local leaders on the evening of the same day to discuss solutions. It is unknown how it will be resolved. (June 30)

Company Law and Implementation Law 70

Promulgated and Implemented on July 1st

The Ministry of Industry stated that the Company Law and Implementation Law have been reviewed and approved by the Legislative Yuan and set by the National Government to be implemented on July 1st. The Ministry issued a decree yesterday and notified all provinces and cities. The text of the articles is recorded as follows:

Chapter 1 General Provisions (Article 1) The procedures for matters that should be registered in accordance with the Company Law and the Company Law Implementation Law shall be in accordance with the provisions of these Rules. (Article 2) The competent authority mentioned in the Company Law is the Department of Industry in the province and the Bureau of Social Affairs in the city under the jurisdiction of the Executive Yuan. (Article 3) Company registration shall be applied for by the party concerned by submitting a petition together with two copies of the documents required by these Rules to the competent authority. When applying through an agent, a power of attorney shall be added. (Article 4) If the competent authority finds that the application for company registration violates the law or does not comply with the legal format, it shall order it to be corrected. Registration shall not be allowed until it has been verified as legal.

(Article 5) Registration of the establishment of a company and the establishment of a branch shall be determined after the Ministry of Industry issues a license. Registration of increased or decreased capital shall be determined after the Ministry of Industry issues a renewed license. (Article 6) The competent authority shall submit the registration of the establishment, dissolution, increase or decrease of capital, and establishment of branches to the Ministry of Industry for approval after approval. The registration of other matters shall be reported to the Ministry of Industry once a month. (Article 7) If the party concerned is sure that there is an error or omission in the registered items after registration, he may apply for correction. (Article 8) The competent authority may, at its discretion, grant a certificate if it is requested to prove that the registered items have not been changed, or that there are no other items registered. (Article 9) The parties concerned or interested parties may state the reasons and request to inspect or copy the register and registration documents, but the competent authority may refuse to copy them or restrict the scope of copying if it deems it necessary.

Chapter 2 Fees (Article 10) When registering the establishment of a company, the license fee shall be paid together with the document according to the following rates: A. Unlimited companies and limited partnerships: 15 yuan for those under 5,000 yuan, 30 yuan for those under 10,000 yuan, 45 yuan for those under 30,000 yuan, 60 yuan for those under 50,000 yuan, 75 yuan for those under 100,000 yuan, 90 yuan for those under 300,000 yuan, 120 yuan for those under 500,000 yuan, 150 yuan for those under 800,000 yuan, 180 yuan for those under 1 million yuan, 225 yuan for those under 1.9 million yuan, 300 yuan for those under 2 million yuan, 375 yuan for those under 3 million yuan, 450 yuan for those under 4 million yuan, and 75 yuan shall be added for every 1 million yuan over 4 million yuan, and those under 1 million yuan shall also be calculated as 1 million yuan. B. Limited companies and limited companies with shares: 30 yuan for those under 5,000 yuan, 60 yuan for those under 10,000 yuan, 90 yuan for those under 30,000 yuan, 120 yuan for those under 50,000 yuan, 150 yuan for those under 100,000 yuan, 180 yuan for those under 300,000 yuan, 225 yuan for those under 500,000 yuan, 300 yuan for those under 800,000 yuan, 375 yuan for those under 1 million yuan, 450 yuan for those under 1.5 million yuan, 600 yuan for those under 2 million yuan, 750 yuan for those under 3 million yuan, 900 yuan for those under 4 million yuan, and 150 yuan shall be added for every 1 million yuan over 4 million yuan, and those under 1 million yuan shall also be calculated as 1 million yuan. (Article 11) If a company applies for registration due to an increase in capital, the license fee shall be calculated according to the total amount of capital after the increase in accordance with the provisions of the preceding article, but the original amount paid at the time of establishment may be deducted. (Article 12) If a company applies for registration to establish a branch, a license fee of 10 yuan shall be paid with the document for each branch. (Article 13) If a company whose head office is not in the territory of the Republic of China establishes the first branch in the territory of the Republic of China and applies for registration, it shall pay the license fee with the document according to the following rates: 1. If the branch does not have a fixed capital, it shall be converted into national currency based on half of the total capital of its head office and paid according to the rate specified in Article 10. 2. If the branch has a fixed capital, it shall be paid according to the rate specified in Article 10 based on its capital amount. (Article 14) If a company whose head office is not in the territory of the Republic of China establishes the first branch in the territory of the Republic of China and is approved for registration, it shall pay the license fee with the document in accordance with Article 12 when it applies for registration to add a branch, but if the added branch has a separate capital, it shall be in accordance with the provisions of Article 13. (Article 15) If a company whose head office is not in the territory of the Republic of China establishes the first branch in the territory of the Republic of China and is approved for registration, and then applies for registration to add a branch, it shall pay the license fee with the document in accordance with Article 12, but if the added branch has a separate capital, it shall be in accordance with the provisions of Article 13. (Article 15) If a company whose head office is not in the territory of the Republic of China increases its capital after the first branch is registered in the Republic of China, the provisions of Article 11 shall apply when applying for registration. (Article 16) The competent authority shall submit the license fee in Articles 10 to 15 of these Rules with the document, but 10 yuan shall be retained for office expenses for each case, and no separate registration fee shall be charged. (Article 17) If a company loses its license and applies for re-issuance, it shall pay a re-issuance

License fee of two yuan. (Article 18) Those who should receive a license in accordance with the law shall pay a stamp tax fee of one yuan with the document. (Article 19) For all company registrations other than establishment and capital increase, a registration fee of five yuan shall be paid to the competent authority for each case. (Article 20) To inspect the register and registration documents, an inspection fee of one yuan shall be paid each time. If a copy is required, a copying fee of five cents shall be paid for each word. (Article 21) For those who apply for a certificate in accordance with Article 8, a certificate fee of two yuan shall be paid for each case. (To be continued)

The Tobacco Suppression and Investigation Office is Established: The Wuxian Tobacco Suppression and Investigation Office has now decided to be established on the 4th. The location will be changed to Siqian Street, and 19 sub-offices will be established in the 19th district. On the one hand, the office will organize an inspection and protection team of 20 people, divided into six-hour shifts. Notorious Bandit Zhu Yubo Sentenced to Death: The notorious bandit Zhu Yubo was previously sentenced to 171 death sentences by the Wuxian District Court. When he was presented to the province for instructions on execution, the provincial government ordered a retrial. The criminal court of the original court repeatedly searched for evidence, questioned the prisoners, and handled the case for years. It was not until the day before yesterday (30th) that the trial was concluded. The verdict has now been handed down, changing the sentence to three death sentences, seven life imprisonments, and deprivation of public rights for life, and one death sentence will be carried out.

Baoshan 73

The County Government Implements Reorganization: Qiu Mingjiu, the Magistrate of Baoshan County, previously received instructions from the Jiangsu Provincial Government that the county had been listed as a third-class county by the Provincial Political Conference and should be reorganized from July 1st. After receiving the order, Magistrate Qiu immediately started the reorganization in accordance with the third-class county system promulgated by the province. As of yesterday, the first and second sections of the county government have been merged into the General Affairs Section, and the original Public Security Section and Secretariat remain as they were. All administrative expenses will also be paid from the budget of the third-class county from today onwards to comply with the system. As the county's original Finance Bureau was deemed unnecessary for a third-class county, it was also ordered by the Department of Finance to be abolished. Yesterday, Director Bei of the bureau had already completed the closing procedures and transferred all files, documents, silver wire accounts, and books to the county government for receipt. The county has set up a Finance Section to directly manage it, and appointed Luo Wenbing, the former Chief of the General Affairs Section of the Finance Bureau, as the Chief of the Finance Section. After the handover, Director Bei immediately took a car to the province to report and take up other positions. Magistrate Qiu has also reported the situation of compliance with the order, reorganization, and receipt of the financial bureau to the provincial department for record.

Wuxi 76

Armed Robbers Wound Accomplice: In the fifth district of the county (Tianshang City), at the home of Zuo Min Yuan Ashi in Nantangtou, yesterday (the 1st) at about 1:00 AM, five armed robbers suddenly arrived. Each held a Mauser pistol. At the time, the men and women of the Yuan family were fast asleep. One robber first climbed onto the roof of Xu Quanbao's house, intending to enter, open the main door, and let the remaining robbers inside. Xu heard the sound of tiles and knew something was amiss. He immediately went out the back door and beat a gong to alert the neighbors. The nearby Zuo villagers heard the gong and came out to capture the robbers. Seeing the situation was not good, four robbers immediately fled. The robber on the roof, seeing his accomplices escaping, panicked. He jumped off the roof and fled after them. The four robbers, suspecting that villagers were coming to catch them, immediately fired their pistols to intimidate them. Unexpectedly, a bullet struck the robber in the back. After being wounded, the robber went to Bantang Temple, lay down on a bench, bleeding profusely and barely breathing. At dawn, the Nantangtou villagers reported to the Public Security Bureau by telephone. Director Xu, upon hearing the report, immediately dispatched Detective Xue Furui and four investigators to the village to pursue the robbers. While passing Bantang Temple, they spotted a person with a gunshot wound whose appearance was suspicious. They immediately went forward to question him. He claimed his name was Qian Hai, from Tongzhou. Yesterday afternoon, he came to Wuxi from Shanghai by train. At the train station, he met four "Red Bandits" who took him to Yuan Ashi's house in Nantangtou to commit robbery, but they were unsuccessful, and he was shot. However, he did not know the names of the "Red Bandits." He claimed he was in the raw silk business. Based on his confession, Detective Xue immediately sent the wounded robber Qian Hai to the city by car and admitted him to the Brothers Hospital for treatment. According to the doctor, the bullet entered from the right back and exited near the right breast, damaging the lungs. Whether it damaged blood vessels was still difficult to determine. The injury was quite dangerous.

County Court Clears Accumulated Cases: Since its establishment in February, the county court has concluded many civil and criminal cases. Four months have passed, and because of the large number of new cases, the old cases have not been completely cleared. Now, starting yesterday (the 1st), accumulated cases will be cleared for five days. Urgent cases involving capital crimes and robbery will be accepted at any time. Also, starting yesterday, court sessions will be held in the morning.

Guo Zhangshi was sentenced to one month's imprisonment and a fine of 500 yuan. If the fines are not paid, one day of imprisonment will be substituted for every three yuan.

Yangzhou 80

Central Committee Member Wang Returns to Beijing After Finishing Business: Wang Bailing, a member of the Central Executive Committee, returned to Yangzhou from Beijing a few days ago for the groundbreaking ceremony of the Xiong Martyr's Garden and Ancestral Hall. He attended the ceremony and instructed the construction team to actively start construction. After finishing his business, he crossed the river south this afternoon (30th) and will take the Beijing-Shanghai train to the capital.

New Twists After Purchasing Sun Yat-sen Memorial Hall Site: The former site of the old City God Temple in this city was previously sold by the Ministry of Finance to demolition contractors. However, various agencies and organizations had previously planned to rebuild it as the Sun Yat-sen Memorial Hall and the County Party Headquarters. Later, it was heard that the Ministry had already sold the site. Subsequently, various agencies and organizations raised the original price and bought it back from the demolition contractors through the county government in order to rebuild it on schedule. It is now heard that the county government has suddenly received an order from the Ministry of Finance forwarded by the Department of Finance, stating that the demolition contractors had filed a complaint with the Ministry, claiming that the resale to the local area was due to coercion. Therefore, the Ministry of Finance instructed the Department of Finance to order the county to investigate and report. After receiving the order, County Magistrate Chen convened a meeting of the members of the Sun Yat-sen Memorial Hall Construction Committee yesterday (30th) to discuss the matter. As a result, the county will prepare a detailed report on the circumstances of the purchase and the payment of the price.

Jiaxing 81

Request to Establish Mobile Grain Tax Collection Point: Citizens of Wangdian Town, Jiaxing, believe that when county government tax collectors go to the countryside to collect taxes, errors and corruption often occur in the calculation of grain taxes. If farmers in rural areas go to the collection point to pay taxes themselves, the travel expenses are uneconomical. Therefore, they visited Yuan Xu, Director of the County Finance Bureau, in the city yesterday to request the establishment of a mobile branch collection point in Wangdian Town to benefit farmers. Director Yuan will consider this and submit it to the province for approval.

Five Rivers Creek Rice Industry Strike: Pan Qinghua, Director of the Third District Office of Wangjiangjing, Jiaxing, went to the Wancheng Rice Shop in the town yesterday to search for opium. He went upstairs and inspected every place and ordered the opening of foreign crates for inspection. Pan then presented two opium bubbles, claiming they were found during the search. However, the rice shop denied that any opium bubbles were found and claimed that silver coins and gold rings were lost. Therefore, the rice shops in the town immediately went on strike and sent representatives Du Juren and Gao Yushu to He to report everything to the County Chamber of Commerce and the Rice Industry Association and request assistance.

Pinghu 82

Approval Granted by County Government to Demolish Imperial Hall: The Imperial Hall of Dezan Temple dates back to the Tang and Song dynasties. The lintels and beams are constructed with large, valuable Phoebe nanmu wood. However, it has been in disrepair for many years and is in a state of disrepair. Now, with the district government having submitted a request to the county government, the Construction Bureau has been instructed to draft a design and hire workers to demolish it immediately.

Telegraph to Province to Remove Dam on Dredged River: The Zhapu District Office is requesting the removal of the soil dam on the Hongni Weir dredged river in the third segment, because it has been there for a long time and is obstructing irrigation of farmland. Yesterday, a district affairs meeting was convened with the heads of villages and assistants, and decided to telegraph the province immediately to transfer the message to the head of the dredging Zhou for immediate strong removal of the dam to benefit agricultural affairs.

Police Chief Embezzles Booty From Mutinying Soldiers: Fang Yisan, a patrol leader from the Zhapu Public Security Bureau, led a search of the mutinying soldiers yesterday, obtaining more than 90 yuan in loot, which he embezzled in full. Upon the knowledge of Lu (blank), the leader of the provincial security team, he was immediately detained, transferred to the county government for legal processing and strict pursuit of the embezzled funds.

Xiaoshan 83

The Great Fire in Heshan Town: Heshan Town in the third district of Xiaoshan is a center for goods from Datong, Zixia, Daqiao, and Shencun, so stores are lined up next to each other. Unfortunately, on the 27th of last month at midnight, the Guanghuo store of Futaixing was carelessly set on fire by a toppled oil lamp, which spread to 34 neighboring stores and residences. Although the four nearby righteousness dragon exerted efforts to extinguish it, it was not easy to put out, and it did not stop until dawn, with losses exceeding 40,000 to 50,000 gold. The essence of the whole town has been reduced by half.

Detailed Investigation of the Fire in Xixing Garage: A fire occurred at the Xixing Highway Automobile Garage in Xiaoshan a few days ago, destroying a total of 13 automobiles, with losses exceeding 20,000 to 30,000 gold. The provincial Construction Office dispatched staff to investigate the cause of the fire at that time. Outside rumours said that the cause was that a staff member reduced the salary, reducing the scale, the staff member after the period submitted a report to the provincial highway director that was not approved, so he poured gasoline all over the car body and set it on fire and burned it. Yesterday, the province sent staff to thoroughly investigate, interrogate and temporarily detain personnel, and take the confession to Hangzhou to return for life.

Anqing 84

Two County Magistrates Removed From Office: At its regular meeting on the 30th, the Anhui Provincial Government passed a resolution to remove Zhang Xiangkun from his post as the County Magistrate of Shou County. Zhu Xianzhi, the County Magistrate of Mengcheng County, will be transferred to take over the post. Ren He (blank) will be appointed as a probationary magistrate to fill the vacated post. Yu Zhou (blank), the County Magistrate of Fengtai County, has been removed from his post and is under investigation. Xia Futang will be appointed as a probationary magistrate to fill the vacated post.

Party and Government Agencies Layoffs and Salary Reductions: Due to the large deficit in the budget for the 20th year of the Republic, party and government agencies will lay off staff and reduce salaries. For example, the Secretariat of the Provincial Government will reduce two clerks in the General Affairs Section of the First Division, one person in the Second Division, four people in the Third Division, one person in the Foreign Affairs Section, two people in the Military Affairs Section, and one person in the Education Section. The Department of Finance will reduce one director and one staff member in each division, for a total of more than ten people. These measures will be implemented starting from July 1st. The other departments, including Civil Affairs, Education, and Construction, will also gradually implement these measures.

Welcoming the Capture of Bandits in Three Counties: Zhou Lao Jiu, also known as Zhou Wangsong, a notorious bandit in Guiqiu Dong three counties, has recently been hiding in Shanghai. The Huaining County Government obtained information and telegraphed the Shanghai Public Security Bureau to arrest him at his address. Now, the county government has dispatched Captain Wang to Shanghai to escort him back to the county for interrogation.

Hefei 85

Grand Meeting to Welcome Chairman Chen: At 2:00 PM on the 26th, a joint meeting of party, government, military, police, agricultural, commercial, academic, women's, and news organizations was held in the auditorium of the County Party Headquarters to welcome Chairman Chen. At 1:50 PM, Chairman Chen, accompanied by Li Erkang, Chief of Staff of the General Headquarters, and Li Mei, Deputy Commander of the 46th Division, arrived by car. At the appointed time, the meeting began. Lei Bin, Chairman of the County Reorganization Committee, delivered a welcome speech, saying that Chairman Chen's tour of inspection was marked by his order to local areas to refrain from entertaining, showing solicitude for the people's hardships, and attentiveness to every detail. However, the counties of Huoqiu, Liuan, and Huoshan were ravaged by communist bandits, which was painful to hear. Hefei was also affected. He hoped that Chairman Chen would wipe out the communist bandits during his tour of Liuhuo and relieve the people of the counties from their suffering. Subsequently, Chairman Chen gave a speech, saying that the Guangdong incident would be resolved by the central government with political means. Zhang Ji had gone to Guangdong to mediate, and there was no problem. However, the spread of communist bandits was a great scourge. He was determined to wipe out the communist bandits completely during this inspection and to reorganize the politics and party affairs of the counties. He hoped that all sectors would assist in order to benefit the future. Liu Junyao spoke on behalf of various sectors, expressing their acceptance of the speech. The meeting adjourned at 4:00 PM after a group photo. At 5:00 PM, various sectors hosted a public banquet for Chairman Chen and his entourage at the Red Swastika Society. Toasts were exchanged until 8:00 PM.

News Briefs in Education

Weng Wenhao Temporarily Acts as President of Tsinghua 86

Wu Nanxuan Resigns Due to Summer Illness, Resignation Rejected

Nanjing, 1st Dispatch: Wu Nanxuan, President of Tsinghua University, has repeatedly submitted his resignation since the school's turmoil. The Ministry of Education has repeatedly rejected his resignation. Recently, Wu personally came to the capital because of the heat of summer and frequent summer illnesses and went to the Ministry of Education to resign in person. Li Shuhua personally rejected Wu's resignation and instructed that he be retained. However, Wu repeatedly stated that his body was not strong enough to bear the heavy workload. Therefore, the Ministry telegraphed Weng Wenhao to temporarily act as president so that Wu could temporarily reduce the heavy workload and recuperate. The instructions to retain Wu and the telegram to appoint Weng are recorded below: First, instructions to retain Wu: We have received the report. The president of the school previously submitted his resignation, and this Ministry instructed that he be retained and ordered to continue to be responsible. Now, according to the report, he has worked hard to maintain the school for a month. The heat of summer and the frequent summer illnesses show that he values his duties and is deeply concerned. However, school affairs are important and depend on his leadership. The president has been appointed and should not be quick to retire. The claim that his body is weak and needs to be recuperated is true. The Ministry has telegraphed Weng Wenhao to temporarily act as president so that the president can temporarily reduce the heavy workload and recuperate. The request for resignation should not be discussed. The telegram to appoint Weng reads, "Tsinghua University President Wu Nanxuan continues to request resignation due to summer illnesses and inability to bear the heavy workload. This Ministry has instructed that he be retained. However, because the president's body needs to be recuperated, the school's affairs cannot be handled as usual. You are hereby ordered to send someone to temporarily act as president. You must go to the school to take office and report." Seal of the Ministry of Education.

Nanjing, 1st Dispatch: Three representatives of Labor University students, including Liu Peiqian, have arrived in Beijing to request that the central government, the National Government, and the Ministry of Education revoke the order to stop enrollment at the school this year and to meet with Wu Jingheng, the founder of the school, to request assistance.

All Christian Objectives Should Be Removed After the Reclaiming of Church Schools in Zhejiang 88

The Ministry of Education, according to the Zhejiang Education Department's report regarding the matter of whether to include a line in the establishment matters that reads "the spirit of Christ's sacrifice and service" for most church schools, asked for an indication of compliance etc. (The Province of Zhejiang has a total of more than forty private middle schools, of which more than ten were established by churches, including those run by foreigners. The Education Department has already followed the Regulations for Reclaiming Educational Enterprises Run by Foreigners in Zhejiang Province, formulated by the former National Zhejiang University, ordering them to be handed over to Chinese people, to organize a board of directors, and to register in accordance with the Private School Regulations. All of its curriculum must conform to the standards set by the Ministry. Religion may not be a required subject, nor may religious propaganda be carried out in classes. If there are religious ceremonies in the school, students may not be forced or encouraged to participate. Various church schools can also comply with the procedures. However, one point is difficult to resolve, that is, in the establishment matters of the board of directors of various church schools, there is the phrase "the spirit of Christ" or "the spirit of Christ's sacrifice and service". An order has been issued to amend it, and most of it has been amended. However, there are occasional claims that, because of the source of funds, they have no choice but to add this sentence.) The Ministry of Education instructed: "The report has been received. It is said that most church schools in the province are unable to remove the sentence "the spirit of Christ's sacrifice and service" under the establishment purposes because of the source of funds. However, the provincial Department recently submitted the registration form for the Private Yuecai Junior Middle School, which has been amended in compliance with the Ministry's order. The registration form for the Junde Girls' Junior Middle School does not contain the above-mentioned sentence. The difficult situation mentioned in the report should no longer be a problem. You should still examine the situation of each school and enact a law to make them delete the sentence in order to be consistent, and report the handling situation."

Ministry Orders That University Preparatory Courses Should Not Issue Graduation Certificates 89

The Ministry of Education previously, according to the Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau's report on the matter of whether to verify and seal the pre-university graduation certificate as presented by the Private Shanghai College of Political Science and Law (the original report contains the following: "But the pre-university courses of the old system of universities, although the Ministry of Education has limited the time for closure, the pre-university graduates before the closure should be recognized. Where should the graduation certificate be sent for verification, etc."), the Ministry of Education instructed the Municipal Education Bureau: "The report has been received. According to the Ministry's regulations on graduation and completion certificates of schools, university preparatory courses should not issue graduation certificates. If necessary, the school may issue a certificate of completion without verification by the educational administration authority. You should forward this to the school for information." This order.

Record of the International Agricultural Conference (I) 94

(Sent by Mr. Tang Huisun, Chinese Delegate, from Prague, Czech Republic, on June 8)

| Delegates from 31 Countries, More than 1,000 Members... 17 Proposals

The International Agricultural Conference holds a general assembly every two years. The 14th General Assembly was held in Bucharest, the capital of Romania, in 1929. At that time, it was decided that the 15th General Assembly would be held in Prague, the capital of Czechoslovakia, from June 5th to 8th, 1931. Each General Assembly discusses various important proposals related to agriculture in order to solve international agricultural problems. The conference is convened and organized by the International Commission of Agriculture in Paris. Each General Assembly has an organizing committee to prepare all matters related to the General Assembly at the meeting location. In addition to members and representatives of academic groups, the governments of various countries are invited to send representatives to participate in the General Assembly. The government of our country sent me to attend this meeting as a representative. I will briefly record the proceedings of the four-day meeting.

Opening Ceremony of the Conference 95

June 5th was the first day of the General Assembly. The meeting venue was in the Czech Parliament in Prague at 10:00 AM. Representatives from the governments of 31 countries attended, and more than 1,000 people attended, including representatives of academic groups and members. Mr. Qi Zhitang, representative of the New China Agricultural Society, also attended, as the society had already joined the International Commission of Agriculture as a member. Czech President Masaryk and all cabinet members attended in person. The meeting was chaired by Mr. Fuqi, Chairman of the International Commission of Agriculture. First, the Chairman of the General Assembly Organizing Committee and the Chairman of the International Commission of Agriculture gave reports and speeches, followed by a speech by the Prime Minister of the Czech Republic. Then, five Vice-Chairmen of the International Commission of Agriculture, such as Professor Labour of Switzerland, gave speeches. These people are all well-known scholars in the modern agricultural field. Their topics included (1) the status of world agriculture, (2) the International Commission of Agriculture must work with the League of Nations, the International Institute of Agriculture in Rome, and the International Labour Office to rescue agricultural fatigue, (3) the international cooperation and mutual assistance of agriculture to rescue agricultural fatigue, (4) agricultural countries in central and eastern Europe must work together to ensure the certainty of sales routes for major agricultural products, and (5) the status of Czechoslovakia as a central European agricultural and industrial country. These are all important issues in international agriculture at present. After the speeches, the General Assembly was presumed to form various organizational proposals, and the chairman and vice-chairman. I was also elected as the vice-chairman of the agricultural education and propaganda group, which shows that the General Assembly also pays great attention to China. The speech at the meeting used French as the standard, and German and Czech were sometimes used. The speeches were broadcasted by radio to various countries around the world, with dozens of copies sent.

Shocking News from the World Tennis Tournament 98

| British Women's Champion Loses Again | All Singles Players Eliminated

| Women's Singles Quarterfinals | Men's Doubles Enter Semifinals

London, 30th: England's disappointment in the Wimbledon tennis tournament's men's singles is now mirrored in the women's singles, which has vanished like a flower in a mirror or the moon in water. England's top female player, Ms. Nuttall, was eliminated in straight sets by America's Helen Jacobs. The women's singles has now entered the quarterfinals.

Many Surprises, Champion Fails 99

With Nuttall's defeat in the women's singles, the situation has changed dramatically. Nuttall had defeated America's top female player, Mrs. Harper, twice, while Harper had beaten Helen. Now Helen has defeated Nuttall 6-2, 6-3. This year's Wimbledon can truly be said to be full of surprises.

British Women's Singles Hope Extinguished 100

England's disappointment in the women's singles is not limited to this. Ms. Lungeunt was also defeated by Germany's Krawinkel, and Ms. Schreven was defeated by France's Mrs. Mansou. Hope has been completely extinguished.

Intense Battle in Japanese-Indian Doubles 103

The victory of Japan's Sato Jiro and Kawachi over India's Kerajef and Hedi was very interesting. The Japanese players' cunning and the Indian players' power attracted the audience. The Japanese players' deadly shots and the Indian players' tireless long battles. The Japanese players took a 4-1 lead in the first set. The Indian players hoped to sigh at the fierce shots and pressure in the middle. The Indian players chased to 4-5, but still lost. Kawachi's volley, in the second set, a game was tied three times. The Japanese players' astonishing accuracy resulted in another 6-2 victory. Indian Kerajef's serve was the only way to score points, but the Japanese players' baseline attacks made the Indian players flee far away.

National Tennis Tournament in the Works 106

Scheduled During the National Games

National Rankings to be Determined Simultaneously

Chinese tennis has been lacking in vitality recently, and few promising new players have emerged. The reason for this is that there are very few competitions, and good talent is buried. More importantly, there are no national tennis rankings to date. No one knows who is the best player. Two years ago, during the Qiu Lin competition, disputes arose suddenly. Those who supported Lin said that Lin should be the top player, while those who supported Qiu said that Qiu was the champion of the competition. Therefore, according to unofficial sources, those in charge of tennis competitions are currently planning to hold a national tennis tournament as a matter of urgency. However, the time around the National Games is most suitable, as players from all regions are gathered in one place, which is convenient for both. At the same time, the rankings of national tennis players will be determined.

Chinese Tennis Association Prepares to Participate in the Lawn Tennis Association 107

Talent Being Selected

The Chinese Tennis Association has registered to participate in the Class A competition of this year's Lawn Tennis Association, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. However, a total of ten players are required, i.e., five doubles. Currently, the players to participate are being considered, in order to compete against foreigners in Hangzhou. The performance of the players participating in the open doubles will be used as a reference standard.

Jiangnan Track and Field Team Arrives in Tianjin 108

Resting Today... Competition the Day After Tomorrow

(Tianjin) The Jiangnan Track and Field Team, consisting of 26 people, arrived in Tianjin at 9:00 PM on the 30th, after taking the second train from Nanjing. The Sports Association sent personnel to the station to welcome the team members, who stayed at Nankai Middle School for a day of rest. The Sports Association scheduled a welcome banquet at the Dahua Hotel on the 2nd. The city has been raining for several days. It is scheduled to compete with Tianjin athletes at the Nankai Stadium on the afternoon of the 4th, including 100 meters, 200 meters, 400 meters, 800 meters, 1500 meters, 10,000 meters, 100-meter hurdles, 400-meter hurdles, 16-pound shot put, discus throw, javelin throw, triple jump, long jump, high jump, and pole vault. On the 4th and 5th, they will visit various schools and factories. On the 6th, they will go to Peiping, and on the 12th, they will go to Shenyang, then transfer to Dalian and return to Shanghai. Shanghai's Seventh Representative Congress Opened Yesterday 109

Opening Report on Party, Government, and Military Work in the Morning

Forty-Two Candidate Committee Members Elected in the Afternoon

The Seventh Representative Congress of the Kuomintang's Shanghai Special Municipality was held yesterday (July 1st) at 8:00 AM in the auditorium of the Municipal Party Headquarters. 68 representatives attended (list in yesterday's newspaper), and more than 100 people attended as observers, including Central Executive Committee representatives Zhang Yuejun, Mayor Zhang of the Municipal Government, Gu Gaodi representing the Garrison Headquarters, Wu Jiayu, the Central Organization Department's election supervisor, and all members of the Municipal Executive and Supervisory Committees. After playing music to open the meeting, a presidium was elected. In addition to Pan Gongzhan and Wang Yansong, who were nominated by the Municipal Executive and Supervisory Committees in advance, Wu Kaixian, Chen Junyi, and Du Gang were publicly elected by the Congress representatives to serve as chairmen. After the presidium took their seats, the ceremony was performed (opening ceremony in yesterday's newspaper). After the opening ceremony, photos were taken and lunch was served. In the afternoon, the meeting continued to elect the Executive and Supervisory Committee members, and various committees held separate meetings. In the evening, the Municipal Executive Committee hosted a banquet for all representatives. It is heard that the meeting will continue tomorrow to discuss various proposals. The details obtained yesterday are recorded as follows:

Morning Opening Ceremony 110

Assembly Staff: Chairman Group: Pan Gongzhan, Wang Yansong, Wu Kaixian, Chen Junyi, Du Gang; Secretary-General: Tao Baichuan; Master of Ceremonies: Xu Yefu; Recorders: Chen Boxiu, Li Jiran; Signature Desk: Chen Jianzong, Shi Shaohua, Dong Junzhu; Reception: Lin Meiyan, Li Shiyong.

(Photo by Wang Kai) Opening Ceremony of the 7th Shanghai Municipal Congress of the Chinese Nationalist Party

Chairman's Report: Chairman Pan Gongzhan delivered the opening address, stating, in brief: Central representatives, representatives of various organizations, esteemed guests, and comrades, today the 7th Shanghai Special Municipality Congress of the Chinese Nationalist Party holds its opening ceremony here. Regarding the future progress of Party affairs, it is certain there will be a great deal of contribution. Looking back since the closing of the 6th Municipal Congress, it has been over a year. It was originally stipulated that the Municipal Congress should be held annually. However, due to the Central Government convening a National Conference in May this year, and the busy situation of Party affairs in Shanghai, it was unavoidably postponed until now to convene the Congress. This point must first be explained to all representatives. We feel that in the past year, the situation of Party affairs in this city has both areas that can bring comfort to all representatives and comrades, and areas that should prompt all comrades in the city to be extremely cautious and apprehensive in the future. What can bring us comfort is that in the past year, the Party, the government, and the people were able to cooperate and cope with the difficult environment, maintaining a stable order in the city. Nationally speaking, in the past year, the rampant reaction of warlords and the harassment of the Red bandits can be said to be unprecedented since the Northern Expedition of the National Revolutionary Army. Our Central Government, based on the teachings of the late Premier Sun Yat-sen, adhering to the principles of our Party, and responding to the people of the whole country, on the one hand, issued a clear order to suppress them, and finally completely eliminated the forces of the reactionary clique, corrected the fragmented and disjointed situation, and completed the great cause of unification again. Then, it devoted all its efforts to the work of suppressing the Red bandits. Shanghai can be said to be a gathering place for reactionary elements. Considering industry and commerce, it is not only the national center but also has very complex international relations. In terms of administration, because the unequal treaties have not yet been abolished and the concessions have not yet been recovered, the progress of all municipal facilities is obstructed everywhere. Fortunately, all comrades in the city were able to work together with one heart and one mind, the Party and the government were able to cooperate, and the Party and the people were able to get along harmoniously. The Party, the government, and the people were able to stand united under the leadership of the Central Government and work together, so that in the past year, the local order was relatively stable, and although industry and commerce were depressed, they did not completely collapse. The Central Government was able to suppress the rebels in the front without being affected in the slightest by the rear in Shanghai. This is the result of the efforts of all Party members and people in the city, and it is also what can make us feel somewhat comforted. However, from another perspective, if we want the Party and the country to be in long-term peace and stability, merely preventing disturbances in a passive way is not a fundamental solution. We must strive for construction work in an active way so that the people can obtain real benefits, only then will there be a solid foundation. In the past, although the Party, the government, and the people were able to cooperate quite well, it seems that they were not able to do so thoroughly enough. This is a point that we should be cautious and apprehensive about and work hard on in the future, to ensure that the Party and the government, the Party and the people in this city are completely united, laying a very solid foundation for construction undertakings. For example, in local autonomy, the citizens still need considerable training. The government should of course take on the responsibility of training, but Party members should also work harder. In any case, we want the people to accept the Party's principles, to be able to exercise the four powers, and to be able to understand the purpose of community-run local autonomy. Only in this way can there be achievements to speak of. Another example is the planned progress of the central urban area, which the municipal government has already decided on, but Party comrades must also assist the government and work hard to promote it to the people, so that the people can understand its great significance and use their spiritual abilities to cooperate with the government, and the construction of the central urban area can be completed as soon as possible. Only when the Party, the government, and the people of this city fully cooperate can they assist the Central Government in completing the great cause of construction during the period of political tutelage. When the Party, the government, and the people can unite and cooperate fully, no matter big or small matters, all internal construction work, the abolition of unequal treaties, and the recovery of concessions, etc., can be accomplished without problems. In the past year, although there was considerable connection between the Party, the government, and the people, it has not reached the point of being sensitive. Reactionary elements must hope that we cannot cooperate fully, only then will they have an opportunity to take advantage of. Therefore, to what extent the Party, the government, and the people can cooperate is the standard for how successful the construction will be in the future. This is what all our comrades should be extremely cautious, apprehensive, and work hard to do. Today, all of you comrades are holding a meeting here. I hope that the central representatives will provide detailed guidance, so that everyone can inherit the Central Government's spirit and work hard for the Party and the country.

Central Instruction: Central Representative Zhang Qun delivered an instruction, stating, in brief: Chairman and representatives, today the Chinese Nationalist Party of the Shanghai Special Municipality is holding its Seventh Municipal Congress. As the highest administrative official of the area, I was originally going to represent the Municipal Government to make a municipal report, but last night I received a telegram from the Secretariat of the Central Committee, saying that I was instructed by the Standing Committee to represent the Central Committee to give a speech today. Therefore, I am now setting aside my position as the local administrative official and first representing the Central Committee to give a speech. Since the Sixth Municipal Congress of the Shanghai Special Municipality Party Headquarters, a year has passed. According to the provisions of the general charter, the Seventh Congress should be held. The powers of the Congress are no more than three points: (1) To accept and adopt the reports of the Municipal Executive and Supervisory Committees and various organizations; (2) To decide on the strategies for the Party affairs of this city; (3) To elect the members of the Municipal Executive and Supervisory Committees. As for how to adopt the reports of various organizations and how to decide on the strategies for the Party affairs of this city, the teachings of the late Premier Sun Yat-sen and the various resolutions passed by the Central Committee before and after should of course be taken as the standards. What has already been done should be further promoted and developed. For what has not been done, for the sake of preventing further losses, the work should be stepped up. According to the previous intentions entrusted by the Central Government, the Party affairs of the Shanghai Special Municipality have a relatively long history and good achievements. In the negative aspect, eliminating reactionaries has been done with all efforts. In the positive aspect, propagating the ideology has been done deeply among the people. This is especially commendable. If it were not for the loving and sincere spirit of the thousands of Party members in the city, united as one and fighting together, how could this have been achieved? I remember the speech of the late Premier Sun Yat-sen at the First National Congress of our Party, saying that the spirit of a political party lies in all the members and in the leaders, and that the struggle of Party members is the same as the struggle of the army. The spirit of all comrades in the Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters is close to this. Today's achievements are by no means accidental. The adverse environment in Shanghai, where people from all directions gather, is definitely beyond what other places can match. As the Chairman said, the concessions are a place where filth is hidden and reactionary elements gather and stir up trouble. This is enough to endanger the Party and the country. Therefore, before the extraterritoriality is abolished and the concessions are recovered, our comrades must work even harder to achieve great results. According to the population survey report of this city, the population of this city has reached 3.15 million. With such a large population, the number of Party members compared to the population is actually a small minority. Moreover, Shanghai is a major center of economy, culture, industry, and commerce, and a place where talented people gather. There is no lack of virtuous people. For the sake of believing in the Party's principles, for enriching the Party's quality and strength, and for completing political tutelage, the recruitment of construction talents is not to be delayed. The Central Government also hopes for this very much. I hope that the Shanghai Municipal Party Headquarters will pay special attention to the introduction of Party members during the recruitment. The future of the Party and the country truly depends on this. More than two years have passed since the closing of the Third National Congress. At that time, in the administrative aspect, the administrative policies and programs were determined based on the teachings of the late Premier Sun Yat-sen. In the military aspect, a plan was also formulated for the creation of troops. Unfortunately, the reactionary warlords attempted to possess the army and become independent. Not only was the creation of troops impossible, but they also rebelled, causing all administrative policies to be impossible to realize. This is truly regrettable. Therefore, the resolutions of the Third Plenary Session of our Party that have been realized in the past two years are truly shameful to speak of. However, we cannot stop doing things because of difficulties. We should work even harder because of the difficulties. The Fourth National Congress will be held three months later. This is giving us an opportunity to review the past preparations. I hope that all representatives of the city will pay attention to this together with all comrades in the city. This is what the Central Government and I hope for.
